After a long day we were hangry and thirsty and having trouble finding a place to eat during covid that was open past ten....  So we called Amarone, and the owner Sandro happened to answer and tell us, come on in until the wine goes dry! Oh boy did we come and let me tell you... Everything was spectacular!! If we could give ten stars we would. If you‚Äôre looking for authentic Italian cuisine this is the place to go.  From the pasta to the dessert it was all perfect üòç The service though... WOW!! Coming from a chef dad who owned restaurants, Sandro the owner is a gem in a pool full of wannabes.  His passion for food with a dab of his fabulous charisma.. what more can you ask for?.  Cant wait to come back!<//review>

It's an ordinary laundromat really, not too dirty nor not super clean. Prices are good too, about $3 for the regular size washer and 25 cents per 5 minutes on dryers. < review>
This is my preferred laundromat in the area, but it does have its shortcomings. There are often unsavory types inside or in the parking lot, and the owners are very upfront about the theft of clothes from the machines on almost a weekly basis; they contend that the responsibility rests on every patron to diligently guard the machines they're using, not with them to provide a safe environment.

The machines are in excellent condition, they are very reasonably priced, and there's never a wait to access them. The seating is a bit uncomfortable and there's no television, but the area is always immaculately clean and usually quiet with a reliable Comcast hotspot nearby. All that coupled with the other excellent businesses found at the Boatyard Shopping Center means I'll probably continue patronizing them on a regular basis.</review>

< Review>
Staff were super friendly and this is a open and airy environment. I loved the vibe.
The food was really good and the only weak point was the house cocktails. They were okay, but for the price...they could have been better (and I'm talking about the flavors...not the strength...the amount of alcohol was fine). This was mid-day on a Thursday (so not very busy)...and it took a while to get our drinks.
Again...two minor knocks....but still a solid 4 stars and we'll go back.< /Review>

<rating>5</rating>< Text>
Fantastic food, great menu selection. Seafood menu that is well priced and really well thought out. The selection is simple and makes for a quality meal.
The interior space is nicely renovated, which fits the menu well. Undersea theme, with fish-scale wall, underwater mural, rose-gold throughout and a patio that is the best in the Riviera.
Nice selection of drinks, from good beers to great spirits for their selection of mixed drinks. Wine selection that complements the restaurant.
Stop by for the crab cakes, which are meaty and not your minced crab so you don't know what your getting. The Ahi poke melts in your mouth.
Can't wait to go back.< /Text>

In excitement I  went there at night one day, I was greeted with a nice lady but she had told me I would have to place an order before I came out, I was so disappointed because I was leaving the next day. < Review>
First time at this place and had a wonderful, authentic mexican meal. We came in around 3:30 on a Monday and were seated right away. Their food was fresh, plentiful, and hot when it arrived. My mom and I shared their sampler margarita flight thing: I forgot the name of it, but fun fact about it; they change the flavors of the sampler tray every time you order it, so it's always a fun surprise! It may seem strange to drink them with that sweet/spicy chili paste they smear on the glass, but it totally tastes better! (Must lick the chilly, it's so good!) LOL
Both our waitress were knowledgeable and friendly. Cozy place to dine in with both small and large groups; highly recommended for real mexican food and dessert. (I had the fried ice cream)</Review>

<GmapID>0x80db7fd0d135ee53:0xc8cbcb444fadc117<//GmapID>< Text>
Wish I could put negative stars. Now, the food was great as far as I made it. Chips and salsa. They serve a nice tasty mild salsa and delicious spicy salsa along with warm crisp homemade chips. I had a drink made by the bartender Mara which was perfect!!! I could tell she's new and in training, but she's a natural. The problem is her management and very unsupportive staff. In fact I do not even think they have management or a GM. There was a suit who was teaching a new drink to the staff, the Summer Vibe I think he called it. Probably is excellent! With the three servers learning the new drink, the bartender watching, the suit, the guy taking pics of food and drinks and some other girl dressed like a bartender, not one person saw the two empty bud light bottles and untouched chips and salsa waisted by the previous patron sitting next to me  along with my empty glass in front of me. I sat there for 40 mins with other employees passing by multiple times. Sadly, it was very slow with only one other person at the bar and a few tables sat throughout the restaurant. Poor Mara did everything, while in her training. No coworkers to help guide her, check on her guests like us servers are supposed to do as a team. There was no management to at least help make drinks and guide her to at least touch the bar top of her guests. She did her best, but a restaurant needs management. Los Pancho needs a true GM to oversee everything and say hi and be welcoming to the guests. I'm sure the food is fantastic like I've heard from many other friends, but with no service you're just a taco shop to go. Now, with The Mexico Cafe in town, Los Pancho's needs to not just step it up, but actually shine and prove themselves. Temecula is a tough crowd. You can either take it as constructive criticism or fail like most restaurants do in this area. Try Los Pancho's for yourself and critique from your experience. With their great tasting food, maybe as guests we can guide the owners to provide a more welcoming experience and less taco shop approach to selling dishes and beverages regardless if it's here for dine in or to go.< /Text>

< review>
I wish I could give zero stars. Arrived and was told it was a 35min wait.. Okay figured it was always busy so would be worth the wait. Finally got seated they have a huge menu and a lot of neat looking drinks. Ordered water while we were deciding on what drink to try. My water cup had lipstick when it was given to me and tasted like dish water. Strike one. Finally decided on our drinks and food. Ordered our drinks and a few moments later the waitress came back told me they were out of the large glasses and she would bring a smaller one. Okay thing happen. After about 1hr 20mins my daughters and I got our food. What about my wife? Waited another 15mins till her food came out. Strike two. Okay by this point we were already kinda frustrated. My burrito had no flavor what so ever and tasted sour. My wife's taco had so much oil it was running out like a waterfall. Strike three. This is the worst restaurant I have eaten at in over 10 years. I would recommend you just stop by Del Taco. I will say our waitress was the best part of the experience.</review>

<rate>5<//rate>< review>
Hubz and I enjoyed a deliciously hearty meal and some scrumptious cocktails for dinner tonight. We started off with a fresh serving of Ceviche which featured fish, shrimp, Octopus, and lemon, topped with thin slices of avocado. It was a large appetizer, but it didn't stand a chance against my hungry hubby and I and was gone in a few short minutes. I sipped on a Casa Amigos margarita that was decked in chile, tajin, and a chile covered mango lollipop that made my entire world go round. For our main course hubz had the ribeye medium rare with corn tortillas which was cooked to perfection. He especially admired how fatty it was and loved how it wasn't trimmed off like at some restaurants. I had the mixed fajitas with flour tortillas that were out of this world. They were soft, warm, and so fresh when they came out even though it was the end of night.

We had a lovely experience and can't wait to be back!! Thank you Los Panchos team your great food and friendly service is greatly appreciated üíñüôåüíñ</review>

<user_name>Dan Vargas< /user_name></record></dataset><record>
< text>
Authentic, cultural atmosphere. Good portions. Good price. Pretty good quality compared to shops of it's calibre. Most locals are aware that a lot of taco shops aren't too far from another in terms of how good they are. There's too many here that are long time features of the SD culinary landscape so most shops over 5 or 10 years old are legit. You'll also find out that each has a particular menu item that is significantly better than the competition too. This one is definitely the spot for surf n' turf fries in the rancho SD area hands down. Consistently good in my experience. El Toro off Meadowbrook offers better surf n turf, but not as consistently. They also offer beer and wine so come with an appetite and leave with an altogether satisfied experience.<//text>

< Review>
We just discovered this bakery recently and we love it!

Everything we tried so far was delicious üòã
Last time we went there we had their Mille Feuille (Napoleon) and Kalb ellouz (Algerian dessert)
